<script> 
    const vbSoLuong = `Số lượng`
    const vbThoiGian = `Thời gian(ngày)`
    const vbThereIsNoShippingInformationForThisProduct = `Không có thông tin giao hàng cho sản phẩm này`
    
    $(document).ready(function () {
        const getDelivery = (id, number) => {
            if (/^\d+$/.test(number) && parseInt(number) > 0) {
                axios.post('/api/UtilsApi/delivery-check', { id, number: parseInt(number), lang: vbLang })
                    .then(function (response) {
                        if (response.data.data) {
                            if (response.data.data.TgGiaoHang.length == 0) {
                                //alert('Sản phẩm này chưa có thông tin về thời gian giao hàng. \nHãy "Cài đặt thông báo"  hoặc liên hệ với BAA để được hỗ trợ !')
                                $('#delivery__order .modal-body').append(`<div class="w-100 fs-5 mt-4 mb-3 text-center text-danger" ><span>Sản phẩm này chưa có thông tin về thời gian giao hàng. <br /> Hãy "Cài đặt thông báo"  hoặc liên hệ với BAA để được hỗ trợ !</span></div>`)
                            }
                            else {
                                renderOrder(response.data.data, parseInt(number))
                            }
                        }
                         else {
                            alert(vbThereIsNoShippingInformationForThisProduct)
                        }
                    })
                    .catch(function (error) {
                        // handle error
                        console.log(error);
                    })
            }
        }

        $('.btn--delivery').on('click', function () {
            const idVatTu = $(this).data('id')
            getDelivery(idVatTu, $('#delivery__order .line_amount_inputs').val())
        })

        const renderOrder = (data, number) => {
            $('#delivery__order .tbody_tblproducts').empty()

                let htmltg = ``
            data.TgGiaoHang.map(tg => {
                htmltg += `<tr >
                                    <th class="">${tg.SoLuong}</th>
                                    <th class="">${tg.ThoiGian}</th>
                                </tr>`
            })
            let tggh = `<table id="OrderProducts" class="w-100 tblproducts" cellpadding="10">
                            <thead class="">
                                <tr class="position-relative">
                                    <th class=" pt-1">${vbSoLuong}</th>
                                    <th class=" pt-1">${vbThoiGian}</th>
                                </tr>
                            </thead>
                            <tbody>
                                ${htmltg}
                            </tbody>
                        </table>`
            $('#delivery__order .tbody_tblproducts').append(`<tr class="line" data-id="${data.ID}">
                    <td class="Symbol w-25 position-relative px-0" ><span class="position-absolute start-50 translate-middle top-0 pt-5">${data.Model}</span></td>
                    <td class="Amount  d-flex">
                        <input class=" px-0 text-center line_amount_inputs form-control" type="text" name="A" value="${number}" size="10" maxlength="10" autocomplete="off">
                        <span class="pt-2 pb-1 px-1">${data.TenDonVi}</span></td>
                    <td class="text-end p-0">
                        ${tggh}
                    </td>
                </tr>`)
        }

        $('.product__detail').on('click', '.btn-delivery--check', function () {
            const idVatTu = $(this).data('id')
            var val = $(`.product__number--value[data-id="${idVatTu}"]`).val();
            $('#delivery__order').modal('show')
            $('#delivery__order .btn--delivery').data('id', idVatTu)
            getDelivery(idVatTu, val)
        })
        $('.product-other-item.btn-delivery--check').on('click', function () {
            const idVatTu = $(this).data('id')
            var dataLog = $(this).data('log');
            $('#delivery__order').modal('show')
            $('#delivery__order .btn--delivery').data('id', idVatTu)
            getDelivery(idVatTu, dataLog)
        })
        $('#delivery__order').on('hidden.bs.modal', function (e) {
            $('#delivery__order .tbody_tblproducts').empty()
            $('#delivery__order .btn--delivery').removeAttr('data-id')
        })

    })
</script>

<script>
    const vbQuantityAvailableInStock = `Số lượng hàng hiện có sẵn trong kho.`
    const vbInstalledNotificationsForThisProduct = `Đã cài đặt thông báo cho sản phẩm này`
    const vbFailedNotificationSettingPleaseTryAgainLater = `Cài thông báo không thành công. vui lòng thử lại sau`

    $(document).ready(function () {
        const setNotification = (id, number) => {
            if (/^\d+$/.test(number) && parseInt(number) > 0) {
                const IsSendMail = $("#notification__push .notification__push--is-send-mail:checked").length ? true : false
                axios.post('/api/UtilsApi/set-notification', { id, SoLuong: parseInt(number), IsSendMail })
                    .then(function (response) {
                        console.log(response.data)
                        if (response.data.skip) {
                            alert(vbQuantityAvailableInStock)
                        } else {
                            if (response.data.data) {
                                $('#notification__push').modal('hide')
                                alert(vbInstalledNotificationsForThisProduct)
                            } else {
                                alert(vbFailedNotificationSettingPleaseTryAgainLater)
                            }
                        }
                        
                    })
                    .catch(function (error) {
                        alert(vbFailedNotificationSettingPleaseTryAgainLater)
                    })
            }
        }

        $('.btn--notification').on('click', function () {
            const idVatTu = $(this).data('id')
            console.log(idVatTu)
            setNotification(idVatTu, $('#notification__push .line_amount_inputs').val())
        })

        const renderNotify = (data, number) => {
            $('#notification__push .tbody_tblproducts').empty()

            
            $('#notification__push .tbody_tblproducts').append(`<tr class="line">
                    <td class="Symbol w-50" style="">${data.Model}</td>
                    <td class="Amount d-flex float-end">
                        <input class="line_amount_inputs form-control w-50" type="text" name="A" value="${number}" size="10" maxlength="10" autocomplete="off"> 
                        <span class="pt-2 pb-1 px-2">${data.TenDonVi}</span>
                    </td>
                </tr>`)
        }

        $('.product__detail,.folder--detail').on('click', '.btn-notification--set', function () {
            const idVatTu = $(this).data('id')
            const Model = $(this).data('model')
            const TenDonVi = $(this).data('unit')

            var dataLog = $(this).data('log');
            var getval = $(`.product__number--value[data-id="${idVatTu}"]`).val();
            var val
            if (dataLog) {
                val=dataLog
            }
            else {
                val=getval
            }
            
            if (utilsClientCheckLogin()) {
                $('#notification__push').modal('show')
                $('#notification__push .btn--notification').data('id', idVatTu)
                renderNotify({
                    Model,
                    TenDonVi
                }, val)
            }
        })
        $('#notification__push').on('hidden.bs.modal', function (e) {
            $('#notification__push .tbody_tblproducts').empty()
            $('#notification__push .btn--notification').removeAttr('data-id')
        })

    })
</script>

<script>

        $('.modulItems').on('click','.btnAddIcon_Favourite',  function () {
            const id = $(this).data('id')
            var val = 1;
            let Address = `14.228.244.187`
            axios.post('/api/UtilsApi/add-to-favorite', { IDVatTu: id, SoLuong: val, Address: Address })
                .then(function (response) {
                    if (utilsApiCheckResponse(response)) {
                        if (response.data.error) {
                            alert(response.data.error)
                        } else if (response.data.data) {
                            showNotiAddToFavorite()
                        }
                    }
                })
        });

        const getSimilarProduct = () => {
            if (vbCate) {
                const inputs = []
                $('.similar-options:checked').each(function () {
                    inputs.push({
                        Name: $(this).data('id'),
                        Value: $(this).val().split(',')
                    })
                })
                const params = {
                    Cate: vbCate,
                    Inputs: inputs
                }
                axios.post('/api/UtilsApi/product-count-by-cate', params)
                    .then(function (response) {
                        $('.similar-count').text(response.data.data)
                    })
            }
        }
        const getAllModelCompare = (status) => {
            axios.post('/api/UtilsApi/get-data-model-compare', { Status: status, Lang: vbLang })
                .then(function (response) {
                    let vbCompare =`So sánh`
                    let vbLinkCompare = `/vn/compare/`
                    if (response.data.length == 0) {
                        if (!$('.show_compare-model').hasClass('d-none')) {
                            $('.show_compare-model').addClass('d-none')
                        }
                        return
                    }
                    if ($('.show_compare-model').hasClass('d-none')) {
                        $('.show_compare-model').removeClass('d-none')
                    }
                    $('.row-items_model').empty()
                    let html_compare_footer = ``
                    let countModel = 0
                    let alowCountModel = 3
                    response.data.map(o => {
                        if (countModel < alowCountModel) {
                            html_compare_footer += `<div class="item_model">
                                                <div class="">
                                                    ${o.HinhAnh != '' ? `<img class="img_model" src="${o.LinkHinhAnh + `160/` + o.HinhAnh}" Title="${o.Model}" alt="${o.Model}" />` : `<img class="img_model"  src="${vbPathImageBAA}nosanphamX.jpg" alt="Bao An Automation">` }
                                                </div>
                                                <button class="model_delete-compare btn-close" Title="Delete" data-id="${o.ID}" type="button" >
                                                </button>
                                            </div>`
                        }
                        countModel += 1
                    })
                    html_compare_footer += countModel > alowCountModel ? `<a class="model_compare-more" href="${vbLinkCompare}" aria-label="model compare">
                                                            <span class="model_compare-more-plus">+</span>
                                                            <span class="model_compare-more-count">${countModel - alowCountModel}</span>
                                                        </a>` : ``
                    html_compare_footer += `<a class="btn btn_compare_modal-footer model_compare-button p-0" href="${vbLinkCompare}" aria-label="${vbCompare}">
                                                        <span>${vbCompare}</span>
                                                    </a>`
                    $('.row-items_model').append(html_compare_footer)
                })
        }

            const pageScroll = (key) => {
                $('html, body').animate({
                    scrollTop: $(key).offset().top
                }, 100);
            }
            $('.c-pip__tab').on('click', function () {
                if (!$(this).hasClass('disabled')) {
                    pageScroll("#feature__metadata--id")
                    const tab = $(this).data('tab')
                    activeTab(tab)
                }
            });
            const activeTab = (tab) => {
                if (!$(`.c-pip__tab[data-tab="${tab}"]`).hasClass('active')) {
                    $('.c-pip__tab').removeClass('active')
                    $('.feature__metadata .feature__metadata--tab').removeClass('active')

                    $(`.c-pip__tab[data-tab="${tab}"]`).addClass('active')
                    $(`.feature__metadata .feature__metadata--tab[data-tab="${tab}"]`).addClass('active')
                    if (!$(`.feature__metadata .feature__metadata--tab[data-tab="${tab}"]`).hasClass('loaded')) {
                        loadContentTab(tab)
                    }
                }
            }
            const loadContentTab = (tab) => {
                switch (tab) {
                    case 3:
                        loadDocument()
                        break
                    case 2:
                        callApi(`/api/UtilsApi/product-lineup?ID=${vbID}&lang=${vbLang}&IDProductSeries=${vbIDP_Product_Series}&offset=${0}`, {}, (res) => {
                            $('.feature__metadata .feature__metadata--tab[data-tab="2"]').empty()
                            $('.feature__metadata .feature__metadata--tab[data-tab="2"]').addClass('loaded')
                            renderProducts(res.data.data)
                        })
                        break
                }
            }
            $('.feature__metadata--tab[data-tab="0"]').on('click', '.morelink', function () {
                if($(this).hasClass("less")) {
                    $(this).removeClass("less");
                    $(this).html(ellipsestext)
                } else {
                    $(this).addClass("less");
                    $(this).html("<i class='px-2 bi bi-chevron-left'></i>")
                }
                $(this).parent().prev().toggle();
                $(this).prev().toggle();
                return false;
            });
            $(`.feature__metadata .feature__metadata--tab[data-tab="2"]`).on('click', `.btn-lineup-more`, function () {

            const callApi = (url, params, callBack) => {
                axios.get(url, params)
                    .then(function (response) {
                        callBack(response)
                    })

            $('.product__number.add').on('click', function () {
                let val = $('.product__number--value').val()
                if (val) {
                    const min = $(this).data("min")
                    const multi = $(this).data("multi") ? $(this).data("multi") : 1
                    if (val < min) {
                        $('.product__number--value').val(min)
                        return
                    }
                    const dif = parseInt(val / multi)
                    if (val % multi != 0) {
                        val = dif * multi
                    }
                    $('.product__number--value').val(parseInt(val) + multi)
                } else {
                    $('.product__number--value').val(min)
                }
            })
            $('.product__number.minus').on('click', function () {
                let val = $('.product__number--value').val()
                if (val) {
                    const min = $(this).data("min")
                    const multi = $(this).data("multi") ? $(this).data("multi") : 1
                    if (val < min) {
                        $('.product__number--value').val(min)
                        return
                    }
                    const dif = parseInt(val / multi)
                    if (val % multi != 0) {
                        val = (dif + 1) * multi
                    }
                    const newval = parseInt(val) - multi
                    $('.product__number--value').val(newval > min ? newval : min)
                } else {
                    $('.product__number--value').val(min)
                }
            })

            $('.feature__metadata__link--download').on('click', function () {
                $('.iframe-document_pdf').empty()

                        query.push(`urlDatasheet=`+ url)
                    }
                    if (url.indexOf('catalog') != -1) {
                        query.push(`urlCatalog=` + url)
                    }
                    if (url.indexOf('manual') != -1) {
                        query.push(`urlManual=` + url)
                    }
                })
                let str = `/${vbLang}/view-pdf/?` + `urlActive=` + url + `&` + query.join('&') + `#zoom=100`

            $('.product__detail').on('click', '.product--order', function () {
                const id = $(this).data('id')
                let val = $(`.product__number--value[data-id="${id}"]`).val();
                let DonViTinh = $(`.product__number--value[data-id="${id}"]`).data('unit').toLowerCase()
                let val_SLToiThieu = $(`.product__number--value[data-id="${id}"]`).data('min')
                let val_SLBoiSo = $(`.product__number--value[data-id="${id}"]`).data('multi')
                let Address = `14.228.244.187`
                if (val_SLToiThieu) {
                    if (val < val_SLToiThieu) {
                        if (vbLang == `vn`) {
                            alert(`Sản phẩm được đóng gói theo số lượng đặt tối thiểu là: ${val_SLToiThieu} ${DonViTinh} (hoặc bội số của ${val_SLBoiSo} ${DonViTinh})`)
                            $(`.product__number--value[data-id="${id}"]`).val(val_SLToiThieu)
                        } else {
                            alert(`Products are packaged in a minimum order quantity of: ${val_SLToiThieu} ${DonViTinh} (or ${val_SLToiThieu} ${DonViTinh} plus multiples of ${val_SLBoiSo} ${DonViTinh})`)
                            $(`.product__number--value[data-id="${id}"]`).val(val_SLToiThieu)
                        }
                        return
                    }
                }
                if (val_SLBoiSo) {
                    if (val % val_SLBoiSo != 0) {
                        if (vbLang == `vn`) {
                            alert(`Sản phẩm được đóng gói theo số lượng đặt tối thiểu là: ${val_SLToiThieu} ${DonViTinh} (hoặc bội số của ${val_SLBoiSo} ${DonViTinh})`)
                            $(`.product__number--value[data-id="${id}"]`).val(val_SLToiThieu)
                        } else {
                            alert(`Products are packaged in a minimum order quantity of: ${val_SLToiThieu} ${DonViTinh} (or ${val_SLToiThieu} ${DonViTinh} plus multiples of ${val_SLBoiSo} ${DonViTinh})`)
                            $(`.product__number--value[data-id="${id}"]`).val(val_SLToiThieu)
                        }
                        return
                    }
                }
                val = val.replace(',', '.') 
                axios.post('/api/UtilsApi/add-to-cart', { IDVatTu: id, SoLuong: val, lang: vbLang, Address: Address })
                    .then(function (response) {
                        if (utilsApiCheckResponse(response)) {
                            if (response.data.error) {
                                alert(response.data.error)
                            } else if (response.data.data) {
                                showNotiAddToCart()
                            }
                        }
                    })
            });

                    let textName = ``
                    $('.similar-options:checked').each(function () {
                        //data[`s${$(this).data('id')}`] = $(this).val()
                        textID += textID != `` ? `;` : ``
                        textID += $(this).data('id') + `:` + $(this).val()
                        textName += textName != `` ? `;` : ``
                        textName += removeAccentsUrl($(this).data('name')) + `:` + removeAccentsUrl($(this).data('value'))
                    })
                    let countParams = 0
                    let arrTextParams = textID.split(';')
                    arrTextParams.map((e) => {
                        let path = e.split(":")
                        countParams += path[1].split(",").length
                    })
                    if ($('.similar-options:checked').length != 0) {
                        data[`params`] = textID + ($('.similar-options:checked').length <= 2 && countParams <= 2 ? `_` + textName : ``)
                    }
                    var url=vbLinkProducts + productsConvertUrlCate(data,vbTenSlugCate)
                    window.open(url, "_blank");
                }
            })

        $(".btn--ask_about_Product").on('click', function () {
            const id = $(this).data('id')
            const idVT = $(this).data('idvattu')
            const model = $(this).data('name')

            if ($('#email_ask').val() && $('#phone_ask').val()) {
                axios.post('/api/UtilsApi/send-ask-product', {
                    ID:id,
                    IDVatTu: idVT,
                    Model: model,
                    UserEmail: $('#email_ask').val(),
                    UserPhone: $('#phone_ask').val(),
                    content: $('#askProduct_txtNoiDung').val(),
                    UserAgent: agent
                })
                .then(function (response) {
                    if (response.data.data) {
                        alert(vbSendAskProductSuccess)
                    } else {
                        alert(response.data.error)
                    }
                })
            }
        })

                })

        $('.btnAddIcon_Cart_NoLogin_CT').on('click', function () {
            const id = $(this).data('idsp')
            const idVatTu = $(this).data('id')
            const val = $(`.product__number--value[data-id="${idVatTu}"]`).val();
            const CoGia = $(this).data('cogia')
            const TonBAC = $(this).data('tonbac')
            const SoLuongBanToiThieu = $(this).data('min')
            if (CoGia == 0) {
                let notiStatus = vbLang == "vn" ? `Hàng chưa có giá, vui lòng liên hệ để được hỗ trợ \nHotline: 0901 575 998` : `Product does not have a price, please contact for support \nHotline: 0901 575 998`
                alert(notiStatus)
                return
            } else if (TonBAC <= 0) {
                let notiStatus = vbLang == "vn" ? `Vui lòng liên hệ để được hỗ trợ \nHotline: 0901 575 998` : `Please contact for support \nHotline: 0901 575 998`
                alert(notiStatus)
                return
            }
            else if (val < SoLuongBanToiThieu) {
                let notiStatus = vbLang == "vn" ? `Đơn giá này áp dụng cho số lượng tối thiểu ${SoLuongBanToiThieu} cái. Liên hệ để được hỗ trợ \nHotline: 0901 575 998` : `This price applies to minimum quantity of ${SoLuongBanToiThieu} pieces. Contact for support \nHotline: 0901 575 998`
                alert(notiStatus)
                return
            }
            $('.btnMuaHangTrucTiep').attr(`data-idsp`)
            $('.btnMuaHangTrucTiep').attr(`data-idsp`, id)
            $('.btnMuaHangTrucTiep').attr(`data-value`, val)

            axios.post('/api/UtilsApi/check-add-to-cart', { ID: id, SoLuong: val })
                .then(function (response) {
                    if (response.data.data == 'ok' && response.data.text == '') {
                        axios.post('/api/UtilsApi/count-sum-order-direct', {})
                            .then(function (response) {
                                $('.countModelInCart').text(`(${parseFloat(response.data)})`)
                            })
                        showNotiAddToCart()
                    } else if (response.data.data || (response.data.data == 'ok' && response.data.text == 'noti')) {
                        let notiStatus = vbLang == "vn" ? `Đã thêm vào giỏ hàng. Đơn giá này chỉ áp dụng cho số lượng ${response.data.SoLuong} cái. Liên hệ để được hỗ trợ \nHotline: 0901 575 998` : `Added to cart. This price only applies to the quantity of ${response.data.SoLuong} pieces. Contact for support \nHotline: 0901 575 998`
                        alert(notiStatus)
                        window.location.href = '/vn/giohang.aspx';
                    } else {
                        if (hasSessionDangNhap == `1`) {
                            let sl = response.data.SoLuong
                            $.ajax({
                                type: 'GET',
                                url: '/services/giohang.ashx',
                                data: { 'action': 'add', 'id': id, 'soluong': sl, 'lang': 'vn' },
                                dataType: 'html'
                            }).done(function (data) {
                                axios.post('/api/UtilsApi/count-sum-order-direct', {})
                                    .then(function (response) {
                                        $('.countModelInCart').text(`(${parseFloat(response.data)})`)
                                    })
                                if (response.data.text == 'noti') {
                                    let notiStatus = vbLang == "vn" ? `Đã thêm vào giỏ hàng. Đơn giá này chỉ áp dụng cho số lượng ${sl} cái. Liên hệ để được hỗ trợ \nHotline: 0901 575 998` : `Added to cart. This unit price only applies to the quantity of ${sl} pieces. Contact for support \nHotline: 0901 575 998`
                                    alert(notiStatus)
                                    window.location.href = '/vn/giohang.aspx';
                                } else {
                                    showNotiAddToCart()
                                }
                            })
                        } else {
                            $('#loginModal').modal('show')
                        }
                    }
                })
        })

            const id = $(this).parents('.widget_Items').data('id')
            if ($(this).val()) {
                const search = removeAccents($(this).val().toLowerCase())
                $(`.widget_Items[data-id="${id}"] .itemLabel`).each(function () {
                    if (removeAccents($(this).text().toLowerCase()).indexOf(search) == -1) {
                        if (!$(this).parents('.widget_Item').hasClass('d-none')) {
                            $(this).parents('.widget_Item').addClass('d-none')
                        }
                    } else {
                        $(this).parents('.widget_Item').removeClass('d-none')
                    }
                })
            } else {
                $(`.widget_Items[data-id="${id}"] .widget_Item`).removeClass('d-none')
            }
        })
        $('.btnAddToCompare').on('click', function () {
            let $this = $(this)
            var id = $this.attr('data-id')
            var status = $this.attr('data-status')
            axios.post('/api/UtilsApi/check-add-remove-to-compare', { ID: id, Status: status })
                .then(function (response) {
                    if (response.data.data == 0) {
                        $this.attr('data-status', 1)
                        $this.attr('title', vbRemoveCompare)
                        $('.icon-add-remove_compare').empty()
                        $('.icon-add-remove_compare').append('<i class="bi bi-dash-circle"></i>')
                        $('.text_compare').empty()
                        $('.text_compare').append(vbAddedCompare)
                        getAllModelCompare(1)
                    } else if (response.data.data == 1) {
                        $this.attr('data-status', 0)
                        $this.attr('title', vbAddToCompare)
                        $('.icon-add-remove_compare').empty()
                        $('.icon-add-remove_compare').append('<i class="bi bi-plus-circle"></i>')
                        $('.text_compare').empty()
                        $('.text_compare').append(vbCompare)
                        getAllModelCompare(1)
                    }
                })
            var data = {
                message: 'message_channel',
                id: id,
                status: status
            }
            channel.postMessage(JSON.stringify(data))
        })
        $('.modulItems').on('click', '.btnAddToCompare-modul-ctsp', function () {
            let $this = $(this)
            var id = $this.attr('data-id')
            var status = $this.attr('data-status')
            axios.post('/api/UtilsApi/check-add-remove-to-compare', { ID: id, Status: status })
                .then(function (response) {
                    if (response.data.data == 0) {
                        $this.attr('data-status', 1)
                        $this.attr('title', vbRemoveCompare)
                        $(`.icon-ctsp_${id}`).empty()
                        $(`.icon-ctsp_${id}`).append('<svg class="i-icon o-icon--small" data-modifier=""><use xlink:href="#compare-icon-active-svg"></use></svg>')
                        $(`.text-ctsp_${id}`).empty()
                        $(`.text-ctsp_${id}`).append(vbAddedCompare)
                        getAllModelCompare(1)
                    } else if (response.data.data == 1) {
                        $this.attr('data-status', 0)
                        $this.attr('title', vbAddToCompare)
                        $(`.icon-ctsp_${id}`).empty()
                        $(`.icon-ctsp_${id}`).append('<svg class="i-icon o-icon--small" data-modifier=""><use xlink:href="#compare-icon-svg"></use></svg>')
                        $(`.text-ctsp_${id}`).empty()
                        $(`.text-ctsp_${id}`).append(vbCompare)
                        getAllModelCompare(1)
                    }
                })
            var data = {
                message: 'message_channel',
                id: id,
                status: status
            }
            channel.postMessage(JSON.stringify(data))
        })
        $('.feature__metadata .feature__metadata--tab[data-tab="2"]').on('click', '.btnAddToCompare_sameSeries', function () {
            let $this = $(this)
            var id = $this.attr('data-id')
            var status = $this.attr('data-status')

                    } else if (response.data.data == 1) {

                        $this.attr('title', vbAddToCompare)
                        $(`.icon-add-remove_compare_${id}`).empty()
                        $(`.icon-add-remove_compare_${id}`).append('<i class="bi bi-plus-circle"></i>')
                        $(`.text_compare_${id}`).empty()

<script>
    $(document).ready(function () {
        $('.btn-openbox-tm').on('click', function () {
            $('#staticBackdrop').modal('show')
            $('.btn-createfolderAPI').data(`reload`, 'true')
            $('.btn-createfolderAPI').data(`type`, vbtype)
        })
        $('.btn-creatfolder-favorite').on('click', function () {
            $('#staticBackdrop').modal('show')
            $('.btn-createfolderAPI').data(`reload`, 'false')
            $('.btn-createfolderAPI').data(`type`, '2') // yeu thich type = 2
        })

        $('.btn-createfolderAPI').on('click', function () {
            
            var _this = this
            if ($('input[name="tentm"]').val()) {
                axios.post('/api/UtilsApi/create-Folder', { type: $(this).data('type'), tentm: $('input[name="tentm"]').val(), motatm: $('textarea[name="motatm"]').val() })
                    .then(function (response) {
                        if ($(_this).data('reload') == 'true') {
                            location.reload()
                        } else {
                            if (response.data.data) {
                                $('.select-folder').append(`<option value="${response.data.data.ID}">[${moment(response.data.data.TgLap).format('DD-MM-yyyy')}]${response.data.data.Ten}</option>`)
                                $('#staticBackdrop').modal('hide')
                                $('.select-folder').val(`${response.data.data.ID}`)
                            }
                        }
                    })
                    .catch(function (error) {
                        // handle error
                        //console.log(error);
                    })
            }
        })
    })
</script>

        function darken_screen(yesno) {
            if (yesno == true) {
                document.querySelector('.screen-darken').classList.add('active');
            }
            else if (yesno == false) {
                document.querySelector('.screen-darken').classList.remove('active');
            }
        }
        function close_offcanvas() {
            darken_screen(false);
            document.querySelector('.mobile-offcanvas.show')?.classList?.remove('show');
            document.body.classList.remove('offcanvas-active');
        }
        function show_offcanvas(offcanvas_id) {
            darken_screen(true);
            document.getElementById(offcanvas_id).classList.add('show');
            document.body.classList.add('offcanvas-active');
        }

                                            }

                                        }

                                            $('.show_compare-model').removeClass('d-none')
                                        }
                                        $('.row-items_model').empty()

                                                            <div class="">
                                                            ${o.HinhAnh != '' ? `<img class="img_model" src="${o.LinkHinhAnh + `160/` + o.HinhAnh}" Title="${o.Model}" alt="${o.Model}" />` : `<img class="img_model"  src="${vbPathImageBAA}nosanphamX.jpg" alt="Bao An Automation">`}

                                                            <button class="model_delete-compare btn-close" Title="Delete" data-id="${o.ID}" type="button" >
                                                            </button>
                                                        </div>`
                                            }
                                            countModel += 1
                                        })
                                        html_compare_footer += countModel > alowCountModel ? `<a class="model_compare-more" href="${vbLinkCompare}" aria-label="model compare">
                                                                        <span class="model_compare-more-plus">+</span>
                                                                        <span class="model_compare-more-count">${countModel - alowCountModel}</span>
                                                                    </a>` : ``
                                        html_compare_footer += `<a class="btn btn_compare_modal-footer model_compare-button p-0" href="${vbLinkCompare}" aria-label="${vbCompare}">
                                                                    <span>${vbCompare}</span>
                                                                </a>`
                                        $('.row-items_model').append(html_compare_footer)
                                    })
                            }
                        })
                })

                    getAllModelCompare(1)
                }, 200);

                        let scroll_top = window.scrollY;

                            if (scroll_top < last_scroll_top) {

                            el_autohide.classList.remove('page__header--fixed');
                            document.body.style.paddingTop = 0 + 'px';

            let mainSliderSelector = '.main-slider',

            let mainSliderOptions = {
                loop: true,
                speed: 1000,
                autoplay: {
                    delay: 4000
                },
                loopAdditionalSlides: 10,
                grabCursor: true,
                watchSlidesProgress: true,
                navigation: {
                    nextEl: '.swiper-button-next',

                },
                pagination: {
                    el: '.swiper-pagination',
                },
                on: {
                    init: function () {
                        this.autoplay.stop();
                    },
                    imagesReady: function () {
                        this.el.classList.remove('loading');
                        this.autoplay.start();
                    },
                    slideChangeTransitionEnd: function () {
                        let swiper = this,
                            captions = swiper.el.querySelectorAll('.caption');
                        for (let i = 0; i < captions.length; ++i) {
                            captions[i].classList.remove('show');
                        }
                        swiper.slides[swiper.activeIndex].querySelector('.caption').classList.add('show');
                    },
                    progress: function () {
                        let swiper = this;
                        for (let i = 0; i < swiper.slides.length; i++) {
                            let slideProgress = swiper.slides[i].progress,
                                innerOffset = swiper.width * interleaveOffset,
                                innerTranslate = slideProgress * innerOffset;
                            swiper.slides[i].querySelector(".slide-bgimg").style.transform =
                                "translateX(" + innerTranslate + "px)";
                        }
                    },
                    touchStart: function () {
                        let swiper = this;
                        for (let i = 0; i < swiper.slides.length; i++) {
                            swiper.slides[i].style.transition = "";
                        }
                    },
                    setTransition: function (speed) {
                        let swiper = this;
                        for (let i = 0; i < swiper.slides.length; i++) {
                            swiper.slides[i].style.transition = speed + "ms";
                            swiper.slides[i].querySelector(".slide-bgimg").style.transition =
                                speed + "ms";
                        }
                    }
                }
            };
            let mainSlider = new Swiper(mainSliderSelector, mainSliderOptions);

        function TimKiem() {
            var textSearch = $("#header__search-input").val()
            if (textSearch == "") {
                return;
            }
            textSearch = replaceKeySpecialChar(textSearch) 
            textSearch = encodeURIComponent(textSearch).trim()
            let agent = navigator.userAgent;
            axios.post('/api/UtilsApi/luu-lich-su-tim-kiem', { NoiDung: textSearch, NgonNgu: vbLang, UserAgent: agent })
                .then(function (response) {
                    if (response.data.data) {
                    }
                })
            window.location.href = `${vbLinkProducts}?key=${textSearch}`
        }
        $('.selectlstFavorite').change(function() {
            var val = $(".selectlstFavorite option:selected").val();
            if (val != 0) {
                axios.post('/api/UtilsApi/update-macdinh-folder', { Id: val, Type: 2 })
                    .then(function (response) {
                        if (response.data.data) {
                            $('.linkGotoFavoriteCurent').attr('href', `/vn/chi-tiet-thu-muc.aspx?ID=${response.data.data.ID}`)
                            $('.linkGotoFavoriteCurent').text(`Đi tới ${response.data.data.Ten} (ID-${response.data.data.ID})`)
                        }
                    })
            }
            else {
                $('#staticBackdrop').modal('show')
                $('.btn-createfolderAPI').data(`reload`, 'true')
                $('.btn-createfolderAPI').data(`type`, 2)
            }
          
        });

        $('.show_compare-model').on('click', '.model_delete-compare', function () {
            let id = $(this).data('id')
            let status = 1

            axios.post('/api/UtilsApi/check-add-remove-to-compare', { ID: id, Status: status })
                .then(function (response) {
                    if (response.data.data == 1) {
                        axios.post('/api/UtilsApi/get-data-model-compare', { Status: 1, Lang: vbLang })
                            .then(function (response) {
                                let vbCompare =`So sánh`
                                let vbLinkCompare = `/vn/compare/`
                                if (response.data.length == 0) {
                                    if (!$('.show_compare-model').hasClass('d-none')) {
                                        $('.show_compare-model').addClass('d-none')
                                    }
                                    return
                                }
                                if ($('.show_compare-model').hasClass('d-none')) {
                                    $('.show_compare-model').removeClass('d-none')
                                }
                                $('.row-items_model').empty()
                                let html_compare_footer = ``
                                let countModel = 0
                                let alowCountModel = 3
                                response.data.map(o => {
                                    if (countModel < alowCountModel) {
                                        html_compare_footer += `<div class="item_model">
                                                    <div class="">
                                                    ${o.HinhAnh != '' ? `<img class="img_model" src="${o.LinkHinhAnh + `160/` + o.HinhAnh}" Title="${o.Model}" alt="${o.Model}" />` : `<img class="img_model"  src="${vbPathImageBAA}nosanphamX.jpg" alt="Bao An Automation">` }
                                                </div>
                                                    <button class="model_delete-compare btn-close" Title="Delete" data-id="${o.ID}" type="button" >
                                                    </button>
                                                </div>`
                                    }
                                    countModel += 1
                                })
                                html_compare_footer += countModel > alowCountModel ? `<a class="model_compare-more" href="${vbLinkCompare}" aria-label="model compare">
                                                                <span class="model_compare-more-plus">+</span>
                                                                <span class="model_compare-more-count">${countModel - alowCountModel}</span>
                                                            </a>` : ``
                                html_compare_footer += `<a class="btn btn_compare_modal-footer model_compare-button p-0" href="${vbLinkCompare}" aria-label="${vbCompare}">
                                                            <span>${vbCompare}</span>
                                                        </a>`
                                $('.row-items_model').append(html_compare_footer)
                            })
                    }
                })
            var data = {
                message: 'message_channel',
                id: id,
                status: status
            }
            channel.postMessage(JSON.stringify(data))
        })
